            pca.magento.checkout = false;

            pca.magento.isElementVisible = function( elem ) {

            };

                pca.magento.doLoad();
            };

            pca.on('data', function(source, key, address, variations) {
                
                switch (source) {
                    case "address":
                        if (pca.magento.checkout)
                        {
                            // Because magento is using form validation on each field we need to fire a change on the fields we populate.
                            var provinceField = null;
                            for(var c = 0; c< pca.capturePlus.controls.length; c++){
                                var cont = pca.capturePlus.controls[c];
                                if(cont.key == key){
                                   for(var f = 0; f < cont.fields.length; f++){
                                       var element = pca.getElement(cont.fields[f].element);
                                       if(cont.fields[f].field === '{ProvinceName}'){
                                           provinceField = element;
                                       }
                                        pca.fire(element, 'change');
                                   }
                                }
                            }
                            if(provinceField){
                                pca.setValue(provinceField, address.ProvinceName);
                                pca.fire(provinceField, 'change');
                            }
                        }
                        break;
                }
            });


            var loadHitCounter = 0;
            pca.on("load", function(type, key, control){
                if(type == "capture+"){
                    for(var f = 0; f < control.fields.length; f++){
                        if(control.fields[f].element.indexOf('wait_') == 0){
                            control.fields[f].element = control.fields[f].element.replace('wait_', '');
                        }
                        if(document.getElementById(control.fields[f].element)){
                            //ignore
                        }else{

                            var elementsMatchedByName = document.getElementsByName(control.fields[f].element);

                            if(elementsMatchedByName.length > loadHitCounter){
                                control.fields[f].element = elementsMatchedByName[loadHitCounter].id;
                            }else{
                                control.fields[f].element = "wait_" + control.fields[f].element;
                            }

                            
                        }
                    }
                    control.reload();
                    loadHitCounter++;
                }
            });

            pca.magento.reloadPCA = function() {
                if (console && console.log) console.log("Loading PCA");

340","UZ":"+998","VU":"+678","VE":"+58","VN":"+84","WF":"+681","YE":"+967","ZM":"+260","ZW":"+263"};
                var country = "select[name='country_id']";
                var isdCode = 'div.isdcode .control .input-text';

                /***********ON LOAD******************************/

                Object.entries(countryCode).forEach(([k,v]) => {
                    if($(country).val() == k){
                        $(isdCode).val(v);
                    }
                })

                /*************END********************************/

                /***********ON CHANGE COUNTRY DROPDOWN************/

                $(document).on('change',country,function(){
                    Object.entries(countryCode).forEach(([k,v]) => {
                        if($(this).val() == k){
                            $(isdCode).val(v);
                        }
                    })
                })

                /***************END*******************************/

            }

            pca.magento.loadPCA = function() {

                pca.magento.reloadPCA();
                
                // If you login while in the checkout and add a new address, it will show a popup view.
                var buttons = document.getElementsByTagName('button');
                for (var b = 0; b < buttons.length; b++) {
                    if (buttons[b].className.indexOf('action-show-popup') > -1) {
                        //onclick
                        $(buttons[b]).off('click.pca').on('click.pca', function(){
                            pca.magento.reloadPCA();
                        });
                    }
                }

                // Toggle button for adding billing fields on checkout single step.
                var els = document.getElementsByName('billing-address-same-as-shipping');
                if (els && els.length) {
                    for (var i=0; i < els.length; i++) {
                        //onclick
                        $(els[i]).off('click.pca').on('click.pca', function(){
                            if (this.checked === false) {
                                pca.magento.reloadPCA();
                            }
                        });
                    }                    
                }

                // Logged in user can select an address on billing screen or add a new one.
                var els = document.getElementsByName('billing_address_id');
                if (els && els.length) {
                    for (var i=0; i < els.length; i++) {
                        // onchange
                        $(els[i]).off('change.pca').on('change.pca', function(){
                            pca.magento.reloadPCA();
                        });
                    }                    
                }
                
                if (pca.magento.checkout) {
                    pca.magento.checkUrlChange();
                }
            };

            pca.magento.checkUrlChange = function() {
                if (window.location.href != pca.magento.currentUrl) {
                    pca.magento.currentUrl = window.location.href;
                    window.setTimeout(pca.magento.loadPCA, 500);
                }
                else {
                    window.setTimeout(pca.magento.checkUrlChange, 1000); 
                }
            };

            pca.magento.dynamicMagentoFieldsExist = function() {
                
                var isDynamicRegExp = new RegExp("^[A-Z0-9]{7}$");
                var col = document.getElementsByTagName("*");

                for (var i = 0; i < col.length; i++) {
                    if (isDynamicRegExp.test(col[i].id) && pca.magento.isElementVisible(col[i])) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            pca.magento.doLoad = function() {
                // Load when ready.                  
                if (pca && 
                    pca.platform && 
                    typeof pca.platform.elementExists === 'function' &&
                    (pca.platform.getBindingsForService("PLATFORM_CAPTUREPLUS").length > 0 
                    || pca.platform.getBindingsForService("PLATFORM_MOBILEVALIDATION").length > 0
                    || pca.platform.getBindingsForService("PLATFORM_EMAILVALIDATION").length > 0)
                    && (!pca.magento.checkout || pca.magento.dynamicMagentoFieldsExist())) { 

                    window.setTimeout(pca.magento.loadPCA, 500);
                }
                else {
                    // re-set the timeout
                    window.setTimeout(pca.magento.doLoad, 500);
                }
            };

               
        })(jQuery);
    });
  </script>

        });

        $('body').ajaxComplete(function(event, xhr, settings ) {
            var url  = settings.url;
            if(url.indexOf('checkout/cart/add') != -1){
                setTimeout(function(){
                    var miniCartQty = $('.minicart-wrapper').find('.counter.qty .counter-number').text();
                    miniCartQty = miniCartQty.trim();
                    if(miniCartQty) {
                        var textMyCart = '<span>'+$.mage.__('My Cart')+' ('+miniCartQty+')</span>';
                        $('.customer-menu .header.links').find('li:eq(2) a').html(textMyCart);
                    }
                }, 3000);
            }
        });
    });

       require([
        'jquery',

    ], function($){
        $(function () {
            $(document).ready(function(){
                $('ul.ammenu-items li.ammenu-item.-custom .ammenu-toggle').click(function(){
                   var toogle = '<div class="ammenu-toggle custom-toggle" data-ammenu-js="collapse-trigger" tabindex="0">';
                   toogle += '<span class="ammenu-icon" data-ammenu-js="collapse-indicator"></span></div>';
                   $(this).parent().find('.ammenu-submenu').children().find('section ul li').append(toogle);
                   $(this).addClass('asasas'); 
                   $(this).parent().find('.ammenu-submenu').children().find('section').show();
                   $(this).parent().find('.ammenu-submenu').children().find('section ul li .ammenu-submenu-container').hide();  

                });
                $(document).on('click','.custom-toggle',function(){                    
                    $(this).parent().find('.ammenu-submenu-container').addClass('divactive');
                    $(this).parent().find('.ammenu-submenu-container.divactive').slideToggle();                                     
                });
            });
            
        });        
    });

           <script>
            require(['jquery', 'jquery/ui','slick','mage/translate'], function($){
    var recentViewdPro = localStorage.getItem('recently_viewed_product');
    $('.latest-new-container').css('visibility', 'hidden');
    $('.recent-viewed-container').show();

    var interval = setInterval(checkRecentProduct,300);
    function checkRecentProduct(){
        if ($('.admin__data-grid-loading-mask').css('display') == 'none') {
            setTimeout(function(){
                if($('body').find('.recent-viewed-container .product-item').length) {
                    $('.latest-new-container').css('visibility', 'visible');
                    $('.latest-new-container').hide();
                    $('.recent-viewed-container').show();
						$('.recent-viewed-container .inner-title').hide();
					var dataid = $('.recent-viewed-container').attr('id');
					if(dataid == 'esweb' || dataid == 'deweb' || dataid == 'frweb' || dataid == 'mxweb'){
						   $(".recent-viewed-container .product-items li").each(function(){
								var textdata = $(this).find('.product-item-info .actions-primary .primary span').text();
								if(textdata == 'View More' && dataid == 'deweb'){
									$(this).find('.product-item-info .actions-primary .primary span').text('Details anzeigen');
								}else if(textdata == 'View More' && dataid == 'frweb'){
									$(this).find('.product-item-info .actions-primary .primary span').text('Afficher les détails');
								}else if(textdata == 'View More' && dataid == 'esweb'){
									$(this).find('.product-item-info .actions-primary .primary span').text('Ver más');
								}else if(textdata == 'View More' && dataid == 'mxweb'){
									$(this).find('.product-item-info .actions-primary .primary span').text('Ver más');
								}else{
									$(this).find('.product-item-info .actions-primary .primary span').text($.mage.__(textdata));
								}
							  });
							  if(dataid == 'frweb'){
								$('.recent-viewed-container .product-item-info .publication_date').hide();
								$('.bucket-slider .product-item-info .publication-date').hide();
								$('.tabs-content .products-grid .product-item-info .publication-date').hide();
								$('.latest-new-container .product-item-info .publication-date').hide();
							}   
						}
                } else {
					var dataid = $('.latest-new-container').attr('id');
                    $('.recent-viewed-container').hide();
                    $('.latest-new-container').css('visibility', 'visible');
                    $('.latest-new-container').show();                    
                    if(dataid == 'frweb'){
						$('.latest-new-container .product-item-info .publication-date').hide();
					} 
                }
                clearInterval(interval);

                $('.recent-viewed-container .block-viewed-products-grid .product-items').slick({
                    dots: false,
                    infinite: true,
                    speed: 300,
                    slidesToShow: 3,
                    slidesToScroll: 3,
                    responsive: [
                        {
                            breakpoint: 960,
                            settings: {
                                slidesToShow: 1,
                                slidesToScroll: 1
                            }
                        }
                    ]
                });
                // $('.latest-new-container .block-new-products .product-items').slick({
                //     dots: false,
                //     infinite: true,
                //     speed: 300,
                //     slidesToShow: 3,
                //     slidesToScroll: 3,
                //     responsive: [
                //         {
                //             breakpoint: 960,
                //             settings: {
                //                 slidesToShow: 1,
                //                 slidesToScroll: 1
                //             }
                //         }
                //     ]
                // });

                $(window).trigger('resize');
            }, 700);
        }
    }
});
           </script>
          </div>
